\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    \usepackage[breakable]{tcolorbox}
    \usepackage{parskip} % Stop auto-indenting (to mimic markdown behaviour)
    

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % Keep aspect ratio if custom image width or height is specified
    \setkeys{Gin}{keepaspectratio}
    % Maintain compatibility with old templates. Remove in nbconvert 6.0
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionFormat{nocaption}{}
    \captionsetup{format=nocaption,aboveskip=0pt,belowskip=0pt}

    \usepackage{float}
    \floatplacement{figure}{H} % forces figures to be placed at the correct location
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro

    \usepackage{iftex}
    \ifPDFTeX
        \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
        \IfFileExists{alphabeta.sty}{
              \usepackage{alphabeta}
          }{
              \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs}
              \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc}
          }
    \else
        \usepackage{fontspec}
        \usepackage{unicode-math}
    \fi

    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics
                         % to support a larger range
    \makeatletter % fix for old versions of grffile with XeLaTeX
    \@ifpackagelater{grffile}{2019/11/01}
    {
      % Do nothing on new versions
    }
    {
      \def\Gread@@xetex#1{%
        \IfFileExists{"\Gin@base".bb}%
        {\Gread@eps{\Gin@base.bb}}%
        {\Gread@@xetex@aux#1}%
      }
    }
    \makeatother
    \usepackage[Export]{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size
    \adjustboxset{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}

    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    % The default LaTeX title has an obnoxious amount of whitespace. By default,
    % titling removes some of it. It also provides customization options.
    \usepackage{titling}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage{array}     % table support for pandoc >= 2.11.3
    \usepackage{calc}      % table minipage width calculation for pandoc >= 2.11.1
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines
    \usepackage{soul}      % strikethrough (\st) support for pandoc >= 3.0.0
    \usepackage{mathrsfs}
    

    
    % Colors for the hyperref package
    \definecolor{urlcolor}{rgb}{0,.145,.698}
    \definecolor{linkcolor}{rgb}{.71,0.21,0.01}
    \definecolor{citecolor}{rgb}{.12,.54,.11}

    % ANSI colors
    \definecolor{ansi-black}{HTML}{3E424D}
    \definecolor{ansi-black-intense}{HTML}{282C36}
    \definecolor{ansi-red}{HTML}{E75C58}
    \definecolor{ansi-red-intense}{HTML}{B22B31}
    \definecolor{ansi-green}{HTML}{00A250}
    \definecolor{ansi-green-intense}{HTML}{007427}
    \definecolor{ansi-yellow}{HTML}{DDB62B}
    \definecolor{ansi-yellow-intense}{HTML}{B27D12}
    \definecolor{ansi-blue}{HTML}{208FFB}
    \definecolor{ansi-blue-intense}{HTML}{0065CA}
    \definecolor{ansi-magenta}{HTML}{D160C4}
    \definecolor{ansi-magenta-intense}{HTML}{A03196}
    \definecolor{ansi-cyan}{HTML}{60C6C8}
    \definecolor{ansi-cyan-intense}{HTML}{258F8F}
    \definecolor{ansi-white}{HTML}{C5C1B4}
    \definecolor{ansi-white-intense}{HTML}{A1A6B2}
    \definecolor{ansi-default-inverse-fg}{HTML}{FFFFFF}
    \definecolor{ansi-default-inverse-bg}{HTML}{000000}

    % common color for the border for error outputs.
    \definecolor{outerrorbackground}{HTML}{FFDFDF}

    % commands and environments needed by pandoc snippets
    % extracted from the output of `pandoc -s`
    \providecommand{\tightlist}{%
      \setlength{\itemsep}{0pt}\setlength{\parskip}{0pt}}
    \DefineVerbatimEnvironment{Highlighting}{Verbatim}{commandchars=\\\{\}}
    % Add ',fontsize=\small' for more characters per line
    \newenvironment{Shaded}{}{}
    \newcommand{\KeywordTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\DataTypeTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.56,0.13,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\DecValTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\BaseNTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\FloatTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\CharTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\StringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\CommentTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textit{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\OtherTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\AlertTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{1.00,0.00,0.00}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\FunctionTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.02,0.16,0.49}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\RegionMarkerTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\ErrorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{1.00,0.00,0.00}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\NormalTok}[1]{{#1}}

    % Additional commands for more recent versions of Pandoc
    \newcommand{\ConstantTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.53,0.00,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\SpecialCharTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\VerbatimStringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\SpecialStringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.73,0.40,0.53}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\ImportTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\DocumentationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.73,0.13,0.13}{\textit{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\AnnotationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\CommentVarTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\VariableTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.10,0.09,0.49}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\ControlFlowTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\OperatorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.40,0.40,0.40}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\BuiltInTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\ExtensionTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\PreprocessorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.74,0.48,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\AttributeTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.49,0.56,0.16}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\InformationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\WarningTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \makeatletter
    \newsavebox\pandoc@box
    \newcommand*\pandocbounded[1]{%
      \sbox\pandoc@box{#1}%
      % scaling factors for width and height
      \Gscale@div\@tempa\textheight{\dimexpr\ht\pandoc@box+\dp\pandoc@box\relax}%
      \Gscale@div\@tempb\linewidth{\wd\pandoc@box}%
      % select the smaller of both
      \ifdim\@tempb\p@<\@tempa\p@
        \let\@tempa\@tempb
      \fi
      % scaling accordingly (\@tempa < 1)
      \ifdim\@tempa\p@<\p@
        \scalebox{\@tempa}{\usebox\pandoc@box}%
      % scaling not needed, use as it is
      \else
        \usebox{\pandoc@box}%
      \fi
    }
    \makeatother

    % Define a nice break command that doesn't care if a line doesn't already
    % exist.
    \def\br{\hspace*{\fill} \\* }
    % Math Jax compatibility definitions
    \def\gt{>}
    \def\lt{<}
    \let\Oldtex\TeX
    \let\Oldlatex\LaTeX
    \renewcommand{\TeX}{\textrm{\Oldtex}}
    \renewcommand{\LaTeX}{\textrm{\Oldlatex}}
    % Document parameters
    % Document title
    \title{analysis}
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
% Pygments definitions
\makeatletter
\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}
\def\PY@tok#1{\csname PY@tok@#1\endcsname}
\def\PY@toks#1+{\ifx\relax#1\empty\else%
    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

\def\PYZbs{\char`\\}
\def\PYZus{\char`\_}
\def\PYZob{\char`\{}
\def\PYZcb{\char`\}}
\def\PYZca{\char`\^}
\def\PYZam{\char`\&}
\def\PYZlt{\char`\<}
\def\PYZgt{\char`\>}
\def\PYZsh{\char`\#}
\def\PYZpc{\char`\%}
\def\PYZdl{\char`\$}
\def\PYZhy{\char`\-}

    % For linebreaks inside Verbatim environment from package fancyvrb.
    \makeatletter
        \newbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox
        \newbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox
        \newcommand*\Wrappedvisiblespace {\textcolor{red}{\textvisiblespace}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol {\textcolor{red}{\llap{\tiny$\m@th\hookrightarrow$}}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationindent {3ex }
        \newcommand*\Wrappedafterbreak {\kern\Wrappedcontinuationindent\copy\Wrappedcontinuationbox}
        % Take advantage of the already applied Pygments mark-up to insert
        % potential linebreaks for TeX processing.
        %        {, <, #, %, $, ' and ": go to next line.
        %        _, }, ^, &, >, - and ~: stay at end of broken line.
        % Use of \textquotesingle for straight quote.
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatspecials {%
            \def\PYGZus{\discretionary{\char`\_}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\_}}%
            \def\PYGZob{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\{}{\char`\{}}%
            \def\PYGZcb{\discretionary{\char`\}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\}}}%
            \def\PYGZca{\discretionary{\char`\^}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\^}}%
            \def\PYGZam{\discretionary{\char`\&}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\&}}%
            \def\PYGZlt{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\<}{\char`\<}}%
            \def\PYGZgt{\discretionary{\char`\>}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\>}}%
            \def\PYGZsh{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\#}{\char`\#}}%
            \def\PYGZpc{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\%}{\char`\%}}%
            \def\PYGZdl{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\$}{\char`\$}}%
            \def\PYGZhy{\discretionary{\char`\-}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\-}}%
            \def\PYGZsq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\textquotesingle}{\textquotesingle}}%
            \def\PYGZdq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\"}{\char`\"}}%
            \def\PYGZti{\discretionary{\char`\~}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\~}}%
        }
        % Some characters . , ; ? ! / are not pygmentized.
        % This macro makes them "active" and they will insert potential linebreaks
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatpunct {%
            \lccode`\~`\.\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\.}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\.}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\,\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\,}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\,}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\;\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\;}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\;}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\:\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\:}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\:}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\?\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\?}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\?}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\!\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\!}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\!}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\/\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\/}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\/}}}%
            \catcode`\.\active
            \catcode`\,\active
            \catcode`\;\active
            \catcode`\:\active
            \catcode`\?\active
            \catcode`\!\active
            \catcode`\/\active
            \lccode`\~`\~
        }
    \makeatother

    \let\OriginalVerbatim=\Verbatim
    \makeatletter
    \renewcommand{\Verbatim}[1][1]{%
        %\parskip\z@skip
        \sbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox {\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol}%
        \sbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox {\FV@SetupFont\Wrappedvisiblespace}%
        \def\FancyVerbFormatLine ##1{\hsize\linewidth
            \vtop{\raggedright\hyphenpenalty\z@\exhyphenpenalty\z@
                \doublehyphendemerits\z@\finalhyphendemerits\z@
                \strut ##1\strut}%
        }%
        % If the linebreak is at a space, the latter will be displayed as visible
        % space at end of first line, and a continuation symbol starts next line.
        % Stretch/shrink are however usually zero for typewriter font.
        \def\FV@Space {%
            \nobreak\hskip\z@ plus\fontdimen3\font minus\fontdimen4\font
            \discretionary{\copy\Wrappedvisiblespacebox}{\Wrappedafterbreak}
            {\kern\fontdimen2\font}%
        }%

        % Allow breaks at special characters using \PYG... macros.
        \Wrappedbreaksatspecials
        % Breaks at punctuation characters . , ; ? ! and / need catcode=\active
        \OriginalVerbatim[#1,codes*=\Wrappedbreaksatpunct]%
    }
    \makeatother

    % Exact colors from NB
    \definecolor{incolor}{HTML}{303F9F}
    \definecolor{outcolor}{HTML}{D84315}
    \definecolor{cellborder}{HTML}{CFCFCF}
    \definecolor{cellbackground}{HTML}{F7F7F7}

    % prompt
    \makeatletter
    \newcommand{\boxspacing}{\kern\kvtcb@left@rule\kern\kvtcb@boxsep}
    \makeatother
    \newcommand{\prompt}[4]{
        {\ttfamily\llap{{\color{#2}[#3]:\hspace{3pt}#4}}\vspace{-\baselineskip}}
    }
    

    
    % Prevent overflowing lines due to hard-to-break entities
    \sloppy
    % Setup hyperref package
    \hypersetup{
      breaklinks=true,  % so long urls are correctly broken across lines
      colorlinks=true,
      urlcolor=urlcolor,
      linkcolor=linkcolor,

    \PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{svm\PYZus{}detected\PYZus{}rows} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{detect\PYZus{}using\PYZus{}one\PYZus{}class\PYZus{}support\PYZus{}vector\PYZus{}machine}\PY{p}{(}
        \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,}

    \PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}results}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{resource}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{train\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,}

    \PY{n}{results\PYZus{}table} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{resource}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{data} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{anomalous\PYZus{}values} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{anomalous\PYZus{}values}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}

        \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rows} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{test\PYZus{}anomalous}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{detected\PYZus{}rows} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{method\PYZus{}key}\PY{p}{]}

        \PY{n}{detected\PYZus{}set} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{set}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{detected\PYZus{}rows}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n+nb}{isinstance}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{detected\PYZus{}rows}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{dict}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n+nb}{set}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{detected\PYZus{}rows}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{keys}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{tp} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{row\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{detected\PYZus{}set} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{row\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{anomalous\PYZus{}values}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{fp} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{row\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{detected\PYZus{}set} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{row\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{anomalous\PYZus{}values}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{fn} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{row\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{anomalous\PYZus{}values}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{keys}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{row\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{detected\PYZus{}set}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{precision} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tp} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tp} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{fp}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tp} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{fp}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{k}{else} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
        \PY{n}{recall} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tp} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tp} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{fn}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tp} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{fn}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{k}{else} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
        \PY{n}{f1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{2} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{precision} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{recall}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{precision} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{recall}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{precision} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{recall}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{k}{else} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}

        \PY{n}{results\PYZus{}table}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}
            \PY{n}{resource}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rows}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rows}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{precision}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.3f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{recall}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.3f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{f1}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.3f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{results\PYZus{}headers} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Ressource}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Trainingszeilen}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Testzeilen}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Precision}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Recall}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{F1\PYZhy{}Score}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tabulate}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{tabulate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{results\PYZus{}table}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{headers}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{results\PYZus{}headers}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{STORE}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Store each per\PYZhy{}method table in the tables folder.}

        \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{DataFrame}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{results\PYZus{}table}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{columns}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{results\PYZus{}headers}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}excel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{method\PYZus{}output\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}

    \subsection{Kombinierte Metriken über alle

    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{count\PYZus{}name} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{TP}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{FP}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{TN}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{FN}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{Konfusionsmatrizen (gesamt, Rohwerte)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tabulate}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{tabulate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{confusion\PYZus{}rows}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{headers}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{confusion\PYZus{}headers}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{STORE}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{combined\PYZus{}output\PYZus{}path} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{os}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{join}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tables\PYZus{}dir}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{combined\PYZus{}metrics.xlsx}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{DataFrame}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{combined\PYZus{}table}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{columns}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{combined\PYZus{}headers}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}excel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{combined\PYZus{}output\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}

    \subsection{Autoencoder-Metriken pro
Event-Typ}\label{autoencoder-metriken-pro-event-typ}

Precision/Recall/F1 pro Event über alle Ressourcen. (Ergebnisse nur in
Datei wegen länge)

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{11}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate autoencoder metrics per event type across all resources.}
\PY{n}{event\PYZus{}row\PYZus{}count} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{defaultdict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{event\PYZus{}tp} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{defaultdict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{event\PYZus{}fp} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{defaultdict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{event\PYZus{}fn} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{defaultdict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{resource}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{data} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rows} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{test\PYZus{}anomalous}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{column\PYZus{}names} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{column\PYZus{}names}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{anomalous\PYZus{}values} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{anomalous\PYZus{}values}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{detected\PYZus{}rows} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ae\PYZus{}detected}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{n}{event\PYZus{}columns} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{extract\PYZus{}event\PYZus{}column\PYZus{}indices}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{column\PYZus{}names}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Print and save one FN and one FP}
    \PY{n}{\PYZus{}print\PYZus{}example}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{FN Beispiel}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{examples}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{FN}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{\PYZus{}save\PYZus{}example}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{FN}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{examples}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{FN}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{\PYZus{}print\PYZus{}example}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{FP Beispiel}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{examples}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{FP}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{\PYZus{}save\PYZus{}example}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{FP}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{examples}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{FP}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{STORE}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{Rekonstruktionsbeispiele gespeichert in }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{examples\PYZus{}dir}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Cleanup temporary cached arrays}
    \PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{pop}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}rows\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{pop}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}reconstructions\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{pop}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}rows\PYZus{}reversed}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}

    \subsection{Analyse des originalen Testdatensatzes
(ov\_1)}\label{analyse-des-originalen-testdatensatzes-ov_1}

Bewertung der Anomalieraten im originalen, sauberen Testdatensatz.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{13}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Perform anomaly detection on the original (clean) oven test set.}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{60}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Originaler Testdatensatz (ov\PYZus{}1) \PYZhy{} Anomalieerkennung}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{60}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{oven\PYZus{}resource} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ov\PYZus{}1}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{oven\PYZus{}resource} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}results}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Ressource }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{oven\PYZus{}resource}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ wurde nicht ausgewählt.     \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Visualisierung der Loss\PYZhy{}Historie}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{60}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}files} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{f} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{f} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{os}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{listdir}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}history\PYZus{}dir}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{f}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{endswith}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}loss\PYZus{}history.npy}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}files}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Create individual figures for each resource}

            \PY{n}{resource\PYZus{}id} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}file}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}loss\PYZus{}history.npy}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{60}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{resource}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{data} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{sorted}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{all\PYZus{}results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{key}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k}{lambda} \PY{n}{item}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{item}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{lower}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Get the model for this resource}
    \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{train\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{test\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{n}{val\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{to\PYZus{}numpy\PYZus{}2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{val\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{to\PYZus{}numpy\PYZus{}2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{recon\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{to\PYZus{}numpy\PYZus{}2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{reconstructions}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Reconstruct the original train and validation sets using the already available model pipeline.}
    \PY{n}{\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}reconstructions}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{detect\PYZus{}anomalies}\PY{p}{(}
        \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,}

        \PY{n}{resource}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{redo\PYZus{}hyperparameter\PYZus{}tuning}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{prints}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{val\PYZus{}reconstructions}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{detect\PYZus{}anomalies}\PY{p}{(}
        \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,}

        \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{column\PYZus{}names}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}

        \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{,}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Compute reconstruction errors (MSE per row)}
    \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}errors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}recon\PYZus{}np}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{val\PYZus{}errors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{val\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{val\PYZus{}recon\PYZus{}np}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}errors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{recon\PYZus{}np}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Plot distributions on a log scale for better interpretability.}
    \PY{n}{eps} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{1e\PYZhy{}12}
    \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}log} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{log10}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{clip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{eps}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{val\PYZus{}log} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{log10}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{clip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{val\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{eps}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}log} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{log10}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{clip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{eps}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}log} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{concatenate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}log}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{val\PYZus{}log}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}log}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}linear} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{concatenate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{val\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{bins\PYZus{}log} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{histogram\PYZus{}bin\PYZus{}edges}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{all\PYZus{}log}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{bins}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{40}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{bins\PYZus{}linear} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{histogram\PYZus{}bin\PYZus{}edges}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{all\PYZus{}linear}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{bins}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{40}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} AE threshold (if available in scope)}
    \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{thr\PYZus{}val} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{threshold}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{thr\PYZus{}val} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{None}

    \subsection{Fehlertrennung
(Autoencoder)}\label{fehlertrennung-autoencoder}

Dieser Abschnitt vergleicht die Rekonstruktionsfehlerverteilungen für
normale und anomale Zeilen. Eine größere Trennung deutet darauf hin,
dass Anomalien leichter von normalem Verhalten zu unterscheiden sind.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{17}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Error distributions per resource with boxplots}
\PY{n}{boxplot\PYZus{}tables\PYZus{}dir} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{os}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{join}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tables\PYZus{}dir}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{boxplot\PYZus{}statistics}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{STORE}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{os}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{makedirs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{boxplot\PYZus{}tables\PYZus{}dir}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{exist\PYZus{}ok}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{resource\PYZus{}name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{data} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}array} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{to\PYZus{}numpy\PYZus{}2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{test\PYZus{}anomalous}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{reconstructions\PYZus{}array} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{to\PYZus{}numpy\PYZus{}2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ae\PYZus{}reconstructions}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}array}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{continue}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} compute per\PYZhy{}sample MSE}
    \PY{n}{errors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}array} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{reconstructions\PYZus{}array}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{total\PYZus{}count} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{errors}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} build binary labels array (0 = normal, 1 = anomalous)}
    \PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{zeros}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{errors}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{row\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{anomalous\PYZus{}values}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{keys}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{Exception}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{k}{continue}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{idx} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{idx}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}

    \PY{n}{normal\PYZus{}errors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{errors}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{anomaly\PYZus{}errors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{errors}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{n}{groups} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{normal\PYZus{}errors}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{groups}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Normal}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{normal\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}     
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{anomaly\PYZus{}errors}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{groups}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Anomalie}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{anomaly\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}   

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{groups}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{continue}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create boxplot}
    \PY{n}{fig}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ax} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{subplots}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{figsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{8}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{boxplot\PYZus{}data} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{vals} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{vals} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{groups}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{boxplot\PYZus{}labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{name}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{(n=}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{vals}\PY{p}{)}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{vals} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{groups}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{n}{boxplot} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{ax}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{boxplot}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{boxplot\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{labels}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{boxplot\PYZus{}labels}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{patch\PYZus{}artist}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{widths}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.6}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{colors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Normal}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{C0}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Anomalie}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{C3}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{patch}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{zip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{boxplot}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{boxes}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{groups}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{patch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}facecolor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{colors}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{C7}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{patch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}alpha}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.7}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{median} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{boxplot}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{medians}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{median}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{color}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{darkred}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{linewidth}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} read AE threshold}
    \PY{n}{ae\PYZus{}threshold} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ae\PYZus{}threshold}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{ae\PYZus{}threshold\PYZus{}float} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{None}
    \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{ae\PYZus{}threshold\PYZus{}float} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{ae\PYZus{}threshold}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{isfinite}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{ae\PYZus{}threshold\PYZus{}float}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{ae\PYZus{}threshold\PYZus{}float} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{None}
    \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{Exception}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{ae\PYZus{}threshold\PYZus{}float} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{None}

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{ae\PYZus{}threshold\PYZus{}float} \PY{o+ow}{is} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{ax}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{axhline}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{n}{ae\PYZus{}threshold\PYZus{}float}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{color}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{black}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{linestyle}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{linewidth}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{1.5}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{label}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{AE\PYZhy{}Schwelle}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{alpha}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.8}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{ax}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{legend}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{loc}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{upper right}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{frameon}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{ax}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}ylabel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Rekonstruktionsfehler (MSE)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{fontsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{11}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{ax}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}title}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Fehlertrennung – }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{resource\PYZus{}name}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{fontsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{12}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{fontweight}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{bold}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{ax}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}yscale}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{log}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{ax}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{grid}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{y}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{alpha}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{linestyle}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{tight\PYZus{}layout}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{show}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} prepare summary table}
    \PY{n}{table\PYZus{}rows} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{vals} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{groups}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{q1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{percentile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{vals}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{25}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{median} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{percentile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{vals}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{q3} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{percentile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{vals}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{75}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{iqr} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{q3} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{q1}
        \PY{n}{lower\PYZus{}fence} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{q1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{1.5} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{iqr}
        \PY{n}{upper\PYZus{}fence} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{q3} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mf}{1.5} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{iqr}
        \PY{n}{outliers} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{vals} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{lower\PYZus{}fence}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{|} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{vals} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{n}{upper\PYZus{}fence}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{outlier\PYZus{}share} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{outliers} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{total\PYZus{}count}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{100.0} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{total\PYZus{}count} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nan}

        \PY{n}{table\PYZus{}rows}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}
            \PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{,}

        \PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

    \subsection{Metriken bei
Top-K-Fehlern}\label{metriken-bei-top-k-fehlern}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{18}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Recall, precision, and F1 at top\PYZhy{}k percent of highest reconstruction errors}
\PY{n}{k\PYZus{}percents} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.5}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{\PYZus{}labels\PYZus{}from\PYZus{}anomalies}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}rows}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{anomalous\PYZus{}values}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{zeros}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}rows}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{row\PYZus{}id} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{anomalous\PYZus{}values}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{keys}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{except} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n+ne}{TypeError}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+ne}{ValueError}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{k}{continue}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{idx} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}rows}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{idx}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{labels}

\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{\PYZus{}topk\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{errors}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{k\PYZus{}percent}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{sorted\PYZus{}idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{argsort}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{errors}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{:}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{k\PYZus{}count} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{max}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ceil}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{errors}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{k\PYZus{}percent} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}k} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sorted\PYZus{}idx}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{k\PYZus{}count}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{n}{tp} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{labels}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{top\PYZus{}k}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{total\PYZus{}anomalies} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{labels}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{recall\PYZus{}k} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tp} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{total\PYZus{}anomalies} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{total\PYZus{}anomalies} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{k}{else} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
    \PY{n}{precision\PYZus{}k} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tp} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{k\PYZus{}count} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{k\PYZus{}count} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{k}{else} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
    \PY{n}{f1\PYZus{}k} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}
        \PY{l+m+mi}{2} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{precision\PYZus{}k} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{recall\PYZus{}k} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{precision\PYZus{}k} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{recall\PYZus{}k}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{precision\PYZus{}k} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{recall\PYZus{}k}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
        \PY{k}{else} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
    \PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{recall\PYZus{}k}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{precision\PYZus{}k}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{f1\PYZus{}k}

\PY{n}{recall\PYZus{}rows} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Feature contribution based on per\PYZhy{}column reconstruction error means}
\PY{n}{top\PYZus{}n\PYZus{}features} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}

\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{resource}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{data} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{all\PYZus{}results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{to\PYZus{}numpy\PYZus{}2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{test\PYZus{}anomalous}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{recon\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{to\PYZus{}numpy\PYZus{}2d}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ae\PYZus{}reconstructions}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{per\PYZus{}col\PYZus{}errors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}np} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{recon\PYZus{}np}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}

    \PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}labels\PYZus{}from\PYZus{}anomalies}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{per\PYZus{}col\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{anomalous\PYZus{}values}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{anomaly\PYZus{}idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{where}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{normal\PYZus{}idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{where}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{labels} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{anomaly\PYZus{}idx}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{o+ow}{or} \PY{n}{normal\PYZus{}idx}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{resource}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{: uebersprungen (nicht genuegend Anomalien oder Normalzeilen)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{continue}

    \PY{n}{anomaly\PYZus{}mean} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{per\PYZus{}col\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{anomaly\PYZus{}idx}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{normal\PYZus{}mean} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{per\PYZus{}col\PYZus{}errors}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{normal\PYZus{}idx}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{diff} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{anomaly\PYZus{}mean} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{normal\PYZus{}mean}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Overall mean error across all features (for comparison)}
    \PY{n}{overall\PYZus{}anomaly\PYZus{}mean} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{anomaly\PYZus{}mean}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{overall\PYZus{}diff} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{overall\PYZus{}anomaly\PYZus{}mean} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{overall\PYZus{}normal\PYZus{}mean}

    \subsection{Anomalien je nach der
Zeit}\label{anomalien-je-nach-der-zeit}

Abbildung der Anomalieannzahl und des mittleren Rekonstruktionsfehlers
über die verstrichene Zeit pro Ressource.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{20}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Anomalies over time per resource using the elapsed\PYZhy{}seconds column}
\PY{n}{TIME\PYZus{}COLUMN\PYZus{}KEY} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Property\PYZus{}Current\PYZus{}Task\PYZus{}Elapsed\PYZus{}Seconds\PYZus{}Since\PYZus{}Start}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{n}{TIME\PYZus{}BUCKET\PYZus{}SECONDS} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Set to 60 for minute\PYZhy{}level aggregation.}


\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{\PYZus{}labels\PYZus{}from\PYZus{}anomalies}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}rows}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{anomalous\PYZus{}values}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}

    \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{title}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Anomalien, Rekonstruktionsfehler und Datenmenge je nach der Zeit \PYZhy{} }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{resource}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
